                 <div class="MsoNormal">

                 <div class="MsoNormal">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   To kick off the initial launch of the new platform
                   <a href="http://tabletopready.com/">
                    tabletopready.com
                   </a>
                   which will be a place for Sci-Fi and Fantasy wargamers to
achieve their hobby pursuits were asking gamers whats their hobby story and
to keep them updated when the platform will be open for access for a chance to
win a set of Army Painter Grass Tufts and potential other giveaways to come.
                   <o:p>
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="MsoNormal">
                  <br/>
                 </div>
                 <div class="MsoNormal">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Simply go to
                   <a href="http://tabletopready.com/">
                    tabletopready.com
                   </a>
                   put in your email address and
tell us your hobby story for updates and a chance to win!
                  </span>
                  <o:p>
                  </o:p>

                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Before we go into the services, we want to hear your hobby story? How you got into it, to where you are in your hobby journey today? And, what problems that really irk you ... (we can think of a few right with you.)

                 <b id="docs-internal-guid-cddd1a26-2801-61b3-4ac5-f1e9221f36b3" style="font-weight: normal;">

                 <br/>
                 <div style="text-align: center;">
                  <b id="docs-internal-guid-cddd1a26-2801-61b3-4ac5-f1e9221f36b3" style="font-weight: normal;">
                   <span id="docs-internal-guid-cddd1a26-2801-61b3-4ac5-f1e9221f36b3">
                    <span id="docs-internal-guid-58e878da-28a7-7709-5bf1-21e242ab661c">
                     <span style='font-family: "arial"; font-size: 11pt; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                      <img height="351" src="https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/uJVFpngkM8Zaa37PQxNaYwBqoLFYe1dKMLanPcChGXPVVd7leJakwRTGTDVZjsX2wOT0Ip4JkTLo5h2VBxFtpNkIdgHxMP9UIbmrRMqnR_zTeD9ZpdY1Go-t-Gahd_8FVN6WyIux" style="border: none; transform: rotate(0rad);" width="624"/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </b>
                 </div>
                 <b id="docs-internal-guid-cddd1a26-2801-61b3-4ac5-f1e9221f36b3" style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <br/>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: #38761d; font-family: "arial"; font-size: 30pt; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;'>
                   A Creators Guide
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Content Creator Guide
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    The Role @ Talk Wargaming
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Hello There!
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Before going ahead at full speed read this to get an idea of what Talk Wargaming could use your help with.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                    The Role:
                   </span>
                   <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                    Content Creator
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Content Creator
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Within This Role The Content Creator Will Develop And Create Anything From Written Stories To Videos On Topics He Or She So Chooses Within The 3 Categories.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Payment Structure
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Before you can become apart of our established content creator team we require all prospective candidates to submit a piece of content that is reflected from this guide that will be reviewed by the editors on whether youre quality of content is acceptable to allow you to be on the team or told to try again with a new submission.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <span style="font-size: large;">
                  <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                   <br/>
                  </b>
                  <span style='font-family: "arial"; font-weight: 700; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   Break Down
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Once you get accepted into the team youll then be on the journey that is left entirely up to you on how you wish to progress. Every creator will have the opportunity to build their own personal subscriber base that will in return increase your monetary and special incentives as you become followed on our platform.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Besides special perks youll receive as you become widely followed on our platform the 4 core incentives that will stay with you throughout the entirety of your profile are:
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Bringing in new paying users to the platform.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     These will be the people who will go around and subscribe to creators they like and want to see more of. They pay to be on our platform and do not pay creators directly.
                     <span style='font-family: "arial"; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                     </span>
                     <span style='font-family: "arial"; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                      Everyone you bring onto the platform youll receive 30% of their subscription billing for 1 year.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Example: Subscriber Pays $15 A Month, Youll Receive $4.5 Every Month For One Year Or If The Subscriber Cancels There Subscription Before 1 Full Year, Youll Just Receive Half Up Until The Point They Cancel.
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Per view on your content.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Every time a user views your content youll receive a fixed fee that will grow as your profile subscriber base grows. You can earn a lot more by combining this with #4 on this page.
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Per click each time when someone clicks the button finding your content helpful to their hobby pursuit.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <br/>
                 <h4>
                 </h4>
                 <h3>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large; font-weight: normal;">
                     You will have a monthly goal in comparison to your subscriber base on the platform to bring in a certain amount of new paying subscribers and if you bring in additional people over the monthly goal youll earn an additional $.01 per person after the monthly goal that will be added onto your base per view rate then multiplied by your total views on your for the month. Next month the multiple will be reset to your per view base rate and a new monthly goal to beat.
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <br/>
                 </h3>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Example
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Monthly Goal: 10 Paying Subscribers
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Actually Brought In For The Month: 15 Paying Subscribers
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <ul>
                     <li>
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Per View Base Rate: $.05
                      </span>
                     </li>
                    </ul>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <ul>
                     <li>
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Add an additional $.05 to the per view base rate as 5 additional paying subscribers were brought in over the monthly goal.
                      </span>
                     </li>
                    </ul>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      $.10 X 1000 Views = $100
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 72pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   </span>
                   <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                    Prospective Candidate
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 72pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Submit Either A Battle Report, Story, Tutorial, Or Conversion That Is Created Based Upon This Guide.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Will Be Reviewed By The Editors And Will Either Accept It Or Ask You To Try Again.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="margin-left: 76.5pt;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                   <img height="33" src="https://docs.google.com/drawings/u/0/d/sFaZ1hPMh-GFVnDqBv6o5cw/image?w=26&amp;h=33&amp;rev=1&amp;ac=1" style="-webkit-transform: rotate(0.00rad); border: none; transform: rotate(0.00rad);" width="26"/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Established Content Creator
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: left;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <h2>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Once Accepted Youll Be Apart Of The Team.
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Work On Your Own Schedule.
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Need To Reach 10 Subscribers.
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Incentives Until 10 Subscribers.
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      Youll Receive 50% Of The Subscription Billing From Each Of The First 10 Subscribers You Bring In For One Year.
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      $.01 Per View On Your Content.
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      $.02 Per Click Each Time Someone Clicks The Button On Your Piece Of Content Finding It Useful.
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </h2>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="margin-left: 76.5pt;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                   <img height="33" src="https://docs.google.com/drawings/u/0/d/sCuwysgxvsbIDwHk4d2l12g/image?w=26&amp;h=33&amp;rev=1&amp;ac=1" style="-webkit-transform: rotate(0.00rad); border: none; transform: rotate(0.00rad);" width="26"/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    10 Subscribers
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    After Bringing In Your First 10 Paying Subscribers, Everyone After Youll Be Given 30% Of The Paying Subscribers Billing For One Year.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    $.03 Per View On Your Content.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Content Created When Earning $.01 Per View Will Continue To Earn $.01 Per View.
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    $.04 Per Click On The Helpful Button.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Surpass The Monthly Subscriber Goal And Receive $.01 Per Person To Be Added To Your Per View Base Rate To Then Be Multiplied By Your Total Views On Content For The Month.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: left;">
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="margin-left: 76.5pt;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                   <img height="33" src="https://docs.google.com/drawings/u/0/d/s4hgwp2MJo5Ikkg67nB6Q0w/image?w=26&amp;h=33&amp;rev=1&amp;ac=1" style="-webkit-transform: rotate(0.00rad); border: none; transform: rotate(0.00rad);" width="26"/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    100 Subscribers
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    30% Of The Paying Subscribers Billing For One Year.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    $.04 Per View On Your Content.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Content Created When Earning $.03 Per View Will Continue To Earn $.0.03 Per View.
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    $.06 Per Click On The Helpful Button.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Surpass The Monthly Subscriber Goal And Receive $.01 Per Person To Be Added To Your Per View Base Rate To Then Be Multiplied By Your Total Views On Content For The Month.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: left;">
                  <span style='font-family: "arial"; font-weight: 700; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="margin-left: 76.5pt;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <img height="33" src="https://docs.google.com/drawings/u/0/d/sW-JjnVKcHLUAoF2b3Ty_yg/image?w=26&amp;h=33&amp;rev=1&amp;ac=1" style="-webkit-transform: rotate(0.00rad); border: none; transform: rotate(0.00rad);" width="26"/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    200 Subscribers
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: left;">
                 </div>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Pick A Reward Off Our Hobby List.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="margin-left: 76.5pt;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>

                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: #6aa84f; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Without Further Interruption The Content Creator Guide
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Battle Reports/Campaigns
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Campaigns/Battle Reports should tell an intriguing tale about an army in their quest or pursuit of a objective. The reports should be narrative driven and informative in ways of educating the reader to perform better in their own games.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Educating The Reader In Ways Like These As Example:
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Going over a move you did and why it succeeded or failed.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Explaining why you bring certain units to a game to fight a particular army.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Talk about the terrain in ways on how it benefits your army and doesnt.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Always find ways to help the reader learn new things and improve their own game play.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Content Creator Parameters To Follow:
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Video
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    If The Total Play through Took A Couple Of Hours Then Cut The Video Into 30 - 45 Minute Episodes.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Written
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    What Will Be The Objective?
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    No Less Than 1500 Words.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Every Turn Must Be Detailed On What Happened With You And Your Opponent To Help The Reader Understand The Situation And Learn From It.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    There Must Be Photos, Graphics or GIFs For Every Turn To Visually Demonstrate What Is Going On Within The Battle.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Dont Hesitate To Put In Supplementary Information Or Effects In Graphics To Further Educate And Inspire The Reader.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Stats on the amount of points used.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Photo effects to make it look like there is real combat going on.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    The app LensFX is a great tool for this and only costs $3.00
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Example:
                    <a href="https://i.redd.it/euka3ngxn7vz.jpg" style="font-family: Arial; text-decoration-line: none; white-space: pre;">
                     <span style="color: #1155cc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;">
                      https://i.redd.it/euka3ngxn7vz.jpg
                     </span>

                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Tutorials/Conversions
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.656; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Kinds of Tutorials/Conversions For Any Genre/Game
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    How To Create
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    How To Paint
                   </span>

                 <ul>

                   <span style="font-size: large;">

                   </span>

                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    How To Build
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Starter Guides
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    How To Make
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Content Creator Parameters To Follow:
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Video
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <ul style="margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Have to be edited into 35 - 45 minute episodes if over 1 hour +
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul style="margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Define what type of video it is (Painting, Converting, Building, Etc) and skill level required (Beginner, Advanced, Expert, Master) to let the viewer/reader know what to expect.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Examples
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      For Beginners
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <ul>
                     <li>
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Peter Harrison (The Wargamer)
                       <a href="https://youtu.be/zD90kbrLa_k" style="font-family: Arial; text-decoration-line: none; white-space: pre;">
                        <span style="color: #1155cc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;">
                         https://youtu.be/zD90kbrLa_k

                       <span style='font-family: "arial"; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </li>
                    </ul>

                  </ul>

                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      For Experts
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <ul>
                     <li>
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       Painting Buddha
                       <a href="https://youtu.be/e2G9CEdURNQ" style="font-family: Arial; text-decoration-line: none; white-space: pre;">
                        <span style="color: #1155cc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;">
                         https://youtu.be/e2G9CEdURNQ
                        </span>
                       </a>
                       <span style='font-family: "arial"; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </li>
                    </ul>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Written
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Every step is covered in detail with photos and supplementary information to give the reader a clear understanding of whats involved and how to follow along.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    No cutting corners, go over everything in complete detail for the reader and once you cant describe anymore to further enhance the readers knowledge youll know you're done.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>

                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Content Creator Parameters To Follow:
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Minimum 1500 Words.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    30 min - 45 min segment videos.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    The story must be something along the basis of being funny, incite emotion, debatable, intriguing, or informational, for the reader/viewer.
                   </span>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <li>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Examples:
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/2014/04/n00b-trainer-tips-for-demo-games.html" style="font-family: Arial; text-decoration-line: none; white-space: pre;">
                      <span style="color: #1155cc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;">
                       <span style="font-size: large;">
                        http://www.talkwargaming.com/2014/04/n00b-trainer-tips-for-demo-games.html
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </a>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/2014/10/editorial-kickstarter-kills-gaming.html" style="font-family: Arial; text-decoration-line: none; white-space: pre;">
                      <span style="color: #1155cc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;">
                       <span style="font-size: large;">
                        http://www.talkwargaming.com/2014/10/editorial-kickstarter-kills-gaming.html
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </a>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <ul>
                  <ul>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <span style="font-size: large;">
                      <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/2015/08/army-selection-are-blood-angels-right.html" style="font-family: Arial; text-decoration-line: none; white-space: pre;">
                       <span style="color: #1155cc; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;">
                        http://www.talkwargaming.com/2015/08/army-selection-are-blood-angels-right.html
                       </span>
                      </a>
                      <span style='font-family: "arial"; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;'>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </ul>
                 </ul>
                 <br/>
                 <b style="font-weight: normal;">
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </b>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: #6aa84f; font-family: "eb garamond"; font-size: 20pt; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;'>
                   Hope This Guide Has Given You An Idea Of The Quality And Professionalism We Are Looking For From Content Creators Such As You!
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: #6aa84f; font-family: "eb garamond"; font-size: 20pt; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;'>
                   Look Forward To Reviewing Your Initial Submission.
                  </span>
                  <img height="287" src="https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/XRubcLosscJknbmhfg0yZUEp7lb_jl6lw0WMeyK7f6MVOHhHbUVmvF1JMp7-SWSHKejflHqp50x7Ym9jRzuih3-xi0gtXaUSu8jh_7FoXkpeLbO6asUKrDOf7ATAGiwqawxeicqB" style="-webkit-transform: rotate(0.00rad); border: none; transform: rotate(0.00rad);" width="511"/>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: #6aa84f; font-family: "eb garamond"; font-size: 20pt; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;'>
                   Submit Here: creatorstalkwargaming@gmail.com
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <div style="text-align: left;">
                   <div style="margin: 0px;">
                    <div style="margin: 0px;">
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-size: 11pt; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;'>
                   If you make it on the team we plan on having a idea/suggestion form where creators can contact us 24/7 through email or our personal numbers for any suggestions / ideas to improve any aspect of the platform from creator incentives to the users usability.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.9871999999999999; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "arial"; font-size: 11pt; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre;'>
                   Once Again Look Forward To Your Submission!
                  </span>
                 </div>

                </a>
               </h2>
               <meta content="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-xFcGGryvIr0/WmVAdrnkrNI/AAAAAAAAAIY/xA1oxruxkXAVjNWPJktLyCazBESSlZpkACLcBGAs/s72-c/PaintsSet1.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>

                 <span style='background-color: white; color: #484848; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif; font-size: medium;'>
                  Over the years I have used everything from the cheapest brushes to the most expensive.As a miniature painter one of the most important things in our toolbox are the brushes that we use.
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <span style='background-color: white; color: #484848; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif; font-size: medium;'>
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <span style='background-color: white; color: #484848; font-family: "verdana" , "geneva" , sans-serif; font-size: 12px;'>
                 </span>
                 <div class="separator" style="background-color: white; clear: both; color: #484848; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif; font-size: 12px; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-xFcGGryvIr0/WmVAdrnkrNI/AAAAAAAAAIY/xA1oxruxkXAVjNWPJktLyCazBESSlZpkACLcBGAs/s1600/PaintsSet1.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="color: #2c8b0e; margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em; text-decoration-line: none;">
                   <img border="0" data-original-height="360" data-original-width="640" height="360" original="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-xFcGGryvIr0/WmVAdrnkrNI/AAAAAAAAAIY/xA1oxruxkXAVjNWPJktLyCazBESSlZpkACLcBGAs/s640/PaintsSet1.jpg" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-xFcGGryvIr0/WmVAdrnkrNI/AAAAAAAAAIY/xA1oxruxkXAVjNWPJktLyCazBESSlZpkACLcBGAs/s640/PaintsSet1.jpg" style="border-width: 0px; height: auto; max-width: 100%; transition: opacity 0.2s ease-out;" width="640"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="separator" style="background-color: white; clear: both; color: #484848; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif; font-size: 12px; text-align: center;">
                  <span style='font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif; font-size: medium;'>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif; font-size: 12px; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin: 0px;">
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <span id="goog_1722889029">
                   </span>
                   <a href="https://www.blogger.com/" style="color: #2c8b0e; text-decoration-line: none;">
                   </a>
                   <span id="goog_1722889030">
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="separator" style="background-color: white; clear: both; color: #484848; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif; font-size: 12px; text-align: center;">
                 </div>
                 <div class="separator" style="background-color: white; clear: both; color: #484848; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif; font-size: 12px; text-align: center;">
                 </div>
                 <div class="separator" style="background-color: white; clear: both; color: #484848; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif; font-size: 12px; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-RAaaN4a1RAc/UkDbkHFfyPI/AAAAAAAACwc/zRqJEKkTQVE/s1600/detail_miniature_brushes.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="background-color: transparent; color: #0066cc; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-variant-numeric: normal; margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em; text-decoration-line: none;">
                   <span style='font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif; font-size: medium;'>
                   </span>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <a href="https://www.blogger.com/null" name="more" style="background-color: white; color: #484848; font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif; font-size: 12px;">
                 </a>
                 <span style='background-color: white; color: #484848; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif; font-size: medium;'>
                  Now as you know there are literally hundreds of options out there and I've used many of them over the years that I have been in the hobby.
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <span style='background-color: white; color: #484848; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif; font-size: medium;'>
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                </textarea>
                <div class="post-summary" id="summaryContainer-8994981416087478945">
                 <a class="thumbimgx" href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/2018/03/guide-for-picking-caring-for-your-paint.html" title="Guide For Picking &amp; Caring For Your Paint Brushes">

                 </a>

                   Guide For Picking &amp; Caring For Your Paint Brushes
                  </a>
                 </strong>
                 <p>
                  Over the years I have used everything from the cheapest brushes to the most expensive.As a miniature painter one of the most important thin...

                <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/2018/02/an-introduction-to-airbrushing.html" itemprop="url">
                 An Introduction To Airbrushing
                </a>
               </h2>
               <meta content="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/--hE5gCly4D8/Wqvln463IXI/AAAAAAAAAN8/Z9aw16p41IoeCYfpIny--HQHjB6u_a9fACLcBGAs/s72-c/Airbrushing.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>
               <meta content="2617822810501195147" itemprop="postId"/>
               <meta content="3944947171318631937" itemprop="blogId"/>
               <div class="post-header meta">
                <span class="post-author vcard">
                 <span class="fn">
                  <i class="icon-user">
                  </i>
                  <a href="https://www.blogger.com/profile/02562657979076316608" rel="author" title="author profile">
                   TalkWargaming
                  </a>
                 </span>

                <span class="post-comment-link">

                <span class="post-labels">
                </span>
                <span class="post-timestamp">
                </span>
                <span class="item-control blog-admin pid-477910733">
                 <a href="https://www.blogger.com/post-edit.g?blogID=3944947171318631937&amp;postID=2617822810501195147&amp;from=pencil" title="Edit Post">
                  <img alt="" class="icon-action" height="18" src="http://img2.blogblog.com/img/icon18_edit_allbkg.gif" width="18"/>
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-2617822810501195147" itemprop="description articleBody">
                <textarea id="postData-2617822810501195147" style="display:none;">
                 <div style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "times new roman"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; margin: 0px; text-align: left; text-decoration: none; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;'>
                  <span style="font-size: medium;">
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                 </div>
                 <div style='background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: "times new roman"; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; margin: 0px; text-align: left; text-decoration: none; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;'>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/--hE5gCly4D8/Wqvln463IXI/AAAAAAAAAN8/Z9aw16p41IoeCYfpIny--HQHjB6u_a9fACLcBGAs/s1600/Airbrushing.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                    <img border="0" data-original-height="900" data-original-width="1600" height="225" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/--hE5gCly4D8/Wqvln463IXI/AAAAAAAAAN8/Z9aw16p41IoeCYfpIny--HQHjB6u_a9fACLcBGAs/s400/Airbrushing.jpg" width="400"/>
                   </a>
                  </div>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Hi, Aceldamor here and I wanted to talk to everyone about the infamous device that has appeared in our hobby "The Airbrush"; where do you begin? Its  been a staple tool in the military modeling community for a number of  years, but has only recently become popular in the miniature war gaming realm. Thanks to some of the more popular painters out there via  YouTube, such as
                   <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCTfnfIY3Kyxcv8sWck4sxvQ">
                    Next Level Painting
                   </a>
                   <span style="color: #000032;">
                   </span>
                   ,
                   <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/ThePaintingClinic">
                    Doctor Faust
                   </a>
                   , and
                   <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCDCx2SP6thl7r42CkTdblLA">
                    The War Gamer
                   </a>
                   to name a  few, the airbrush has found a new, and permanent home in our little  community.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <b>
                 </b>
                 <i>
                 </i>
                 <u>
                 </u>
                 <sub>
                 </sub>
                 <sup>

              <article class="post hentry" id="8421943488100390650" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
               <h2 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/2017/12/identifying-your-hobby-play-style.html" itemprop="url">
                 Identifying Your Hobby Play Style
                </a>
               </h2>
               <meta content="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mFifsBW6Ys8/VV4MAwYl1CI/AAAAAAAAAMU/5DYqmGzykGM/s72-c/788px-ChaosRising.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>
               <meta content="8421943488100390650" itemprop="postId"/>
               <meta content="3944947171318631937" itemprop="blogId"/>
               <div class="post-header meta">
                <span class="post-author vcard">
                 <span class="fn">
                  <i class="icon-user">
                  </i>
                  <a href="https://www.blogger.com/profile/02562657979076316608" rel="author" title="author profile">
                   TalkWargaming
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="post-comment-link">
                </span>
                <span class="post-labels">
                 <i class="icon-tags">
                 </i>
                 <span>
                  <span>
                   <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/search/label/Editorial" rel="tag">
                    Editorial
                   </a>

                  </span>
                  <span>
                   <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/search/label/Editorials" rel="tag">
                    Editorials
                   </a>

                  </span>
                  <span>
                   <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/search/label/Fantasy" rel="tag">
                    Fantasy
                   </a>

                  </span>
                  <span>
                   <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/search/label/G" rel="tag">
                    G
                   </a>
                   ,
                  </span>
                  <span>
                   <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/search/label/historical" rel="tag">
                    historical
                   </a>

                  </span>
                  <span>

                    New

                  </span>
                  <span>
                   <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/search/label/Sci%20Fi" rel="tag">
                    Sci Fi
                   </a>
                   ,
                  </span>
                  <span>
                   <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/search/label/Stories" rel="tag">
                    Stories
                   </a>
                   ,
                  </span>
                  <span>
                   <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/search/label/Story" rel="tag">
                    Story
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="post-timestamp">
                </span>
                <span class="item-control blog-admin pid-477910733">
                 <a href="https://www.blogger.com/post-edit.g?blogID=3944947171318631937&amp;postID=8421943488100390650&amp;from=pencil" title="Edit Post">
                  <img alt="" class="icon-action" height="18" src="http://img2.blogblog.com/img/icon18_edit_allbkg.gif" width="18"/>
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-8421943488100390650" itemprop="description articleBody">
                <textarea id="postData-8421943488100390650" style="display:none;">
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mFifsBW6Ys8/VV4MAwYl1CI/AAAAAAAAAMU/5DYqmGzykGM/s1600/788px-ChaosRising.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" height="303" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mFifsBW6Ys8/VV4MAwYl1CI/AAAAAAAAAMU/5DYqmGzykGM/s400/788px-ChaosRising.jpg" width="400"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <span style="font-size: large;">
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <span style="font-size: large;">
                  Whether you are interested in starting a new force, or are trying to maximize your entertainment with a current one, it is a good idea to take a look at your preferred playstyle and see how you can integrate models andtacticsinto your games that will bring you the most fun.
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <span style="font-size: large;">
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                  <tbody>
                   <tr>
                    <td style="text-align: center;">
                     <span style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                      <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/p/identifying-bad-units.html">
                       <img border="0" data-original-height="383" data-original-width="542" height="226" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-JcNSDW3VNX8/WjL30a_NLAI/AAAAAAAAAGY/dkkzxS4EZ_UHpqwCS0nqyke5qoOxP8efACLcBGAs/s320/g2.jpg" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </span>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                   <tr>
                    <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                     <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/p/identifying-bad-units.html">
                      Partnership Message.
                     </a>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                  </tbody>
                 </table>
                 <span style="font-size: large;">
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <span style="font-size: large;">
                  If you're in the market for some new sets, take a look at this, for
                  <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/2017/12/buying-selling-wargaming-miniatures-on.html">
                   buying and selling on eBay
                  </a>
                  .
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <span style="font-size: large;">
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <span style="font-size: large;">
                  Whether you are winning or losing most of your games, if you are doing things you find boring or frustrating during the course of your game, you will get less enjoyment out of the hobby overall.
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <span style="font-size: large;">
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                </textarea>

                 </a>
                 <strong>
                  <a href="http://www.talkwargaming.com/2017/12/identifying-your-hobby-play-style.html" title="Identifying Your Hobby Play Style   ">
                   Identifying Your Hobby Play Style
                  </a>
                 </strong>
                 <p>
                  Whether you are interested in starting a new force, or are trying to maximize your entertainment with a current one, it is a good idea to...
                 </p>
